  <div class="container">
    <div class="row">
      <div class="col-md-6">
                  <h2 style="color:white"><strong>GS1 welcomes APEC&rsquo;s publication on Global Data Standards</strong></h2>

<p>APEC pilots demonstrate that GS1 standards enhance traceability and reduce costs in cross-border trade.</p>
        
                  <div class="item-list"><ul class="list-inline"><li class="first last"><a href="https://www.gs1.org/articles/2336/gs1-welcomes-apec%E2%80%99s-publication-global-data-standards" class="btn btn-margin btn-primary bg-blue">Read the press release</a></li>
</ul></div>              </div>

      <div class="col-md-6">
                              <a href="https://www.gs1.org/articles/2336/gs1-welcomes-apec%E2%80%99s-publication-global-data-standards"
               target="">
              <img  alt="GS1 welcomes APEC’s publication on Global Data Standards" title="GS1 welcomes APEC’s publication on Global Data Standards" class="carousel-image-right visible-lg" src="https://www.gs1.org/sites/default/files/styles/half_width/public/apec-publication-global-data-standards_0.jpg?itok=Wmzv-VSV"/>
              <img  alt="GS1 welcomes APEC’s publication on Global Data Standards" title="GS1 welcomes APEC’s publication on Global Data Standards" class="carousel-image-right visible-md" src="https://www.gs1.org/sites/default/files/styles/one_fourth_width/public/apec-publication-global-data-standards_0.jpg?itok=4flXqnX5"/>
            </a>
                        </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>
        </div>
              <div class="item ">
          <div class="full-width bg-orange">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="row">
      <div class="col-md-6">
                  <h2 style="color:white">GS1 Annual Report 2016-2017</h2>

<p style="color:white">This year&#39;s report is focused on how GS1 helps deliver a seamless end-user experience in today&rsquo;s digital, omni-channel world.</p>
        
                  <div class="item-list"><ul class="list-inline"><li class="first last"><a href="https://www.gs1.org/about/annual-report?utm_campaign=carousel" class="btn btn-margin btn-primary bg-blue">Read our annual report</a></li>
</ul></div>              </div>

      <div class="col-md-6">
                              <a href="https://www.gs1.org/about/annual-report?utm_campaign=carousel"
               target="">
              <img  alt="GS1 Annual report" title="GS1 Annual report" class="carousel-image-right visible-lg" src="https://www.gs1.org/sites/default/files/styles/half_width/public/annual-report-banner-11.png?itok=rGkxCbS1"/>
              <img  alt="GS1 Annual report" title="GS1 Annual report" class="carousel-image-right visible-md" src="https://www.gs1.org/sites/default/files/styles/one_fourth_width/public/annual-report-banner-11.png?itok=iuZ7pToc"/>
            </a>
                        </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>
        </div>
              <div class="item ">
          <div class="full-width bg-blue">
  <div class="container">
    <div class="row">
      <div class="col-md-6">
                  <h2 style="color:white"><strong>Blockchain: GS1, IBM and Microsoft collaborate to leverage standards</strong></h2>

<p>GS1 open standards promote interoperability of blockchain applications across supply chain networks.</p>
        
                  <div class="item-list"><ul class="list-inline"><li class="first last"><a href="https://www.gs1.org/articles/2256/blockchain-gs1-ibm-and-microsoft-collaborate-leverage-standards" class="btn btn-margin btn-primary bg-orange">Read the press release</a></li>
</ul></div>              </div>

      <div class="col-md-6">
                              <a href="https://www.gs1.org/articles/2256/blockchain-gs1-ibm-and-microsoft-collaborate-leverage-standards"
               target="">
